American Psycho | Kokandy Productions | 2023-10-01 | allisforgiven | video

Cast: Kyle Patrick (Patrick Bateman), Sonia Goldberg (Jean), John Drea (Paul Owen), Amber Dow (Mrs. Bateman), Evan B. Smith (David Van Patten), Quinn Kelch (Luis Carruthers), Anna Seibert (Victoria), Emily Holland (Sabrina), Kevin Parra (Sean Bateman), Caleigh Pan-Kita (Evelyn Williams), Hailey Brisard (Vanden), Will Lidke (Timothy Price), Quinn Simmons (Christine), Johnathan Allsop (Craig McDermott), Danielle Smith (Courtney Lawrence), Ryan Armstrong (Detective Donald Kimball)
Notes:
Considering the circumstances, this is a great capture of the Chicago premiere of this show. This production was staged on a runway down the middle of a large room. Audience was seated on both sides of the stage and actors were frequently in all of the aisles. As a result, actors backs are sometimes facing the camera and ensemble actors sometimes obscure the main action in a scene. Because of the layout, it was impossible to capture the entire stage/runway, so only the middle of the runway is filmed. Unfortunately Act Two was very dark so, while most of the action is there, sometimes the picture is less than stellar from the attempt to lighten the footage enough to see anything. Lastly, lots of reactions can be heard from the woman next to me (she was drunk and had several friends in the show so was super vocal). Despite the aforementioned issues, it's a pretty good video and perfectly watchable.
,

Wicked | Broadway | 2004-07-18 | Pigerty | video

Cast: Idina Menzel (Elphaba), Kristin Chenoweth (Glinda), Norbert Leo Butz (Fiyero), Sean McCourt (u/s The Wizard), Carole Shelley (Madame Morrible), Michelle Federer (Nessarose), Randy Harrison (t/r Boq), William Youmans (Doctor Dillamond)
Notes:
This is Kristin and Norbert's last show. It was also supposed to be Joel Grey's last show, but he was ill. Video is sound only for the first 4 minutes and for the last 30 seconds of Defying Gravity. This is a great video with excellent sound. Includes the speech by Idina. This bootleg is a treasure. Multiple copies are circulating. The best is the 7.8 GB file, which has higher video resolution, working menus, and the playbill. The 7.63 GB file has the same video quality but no playbill, skips 1 minute in late Act 1 (A Sentimental Man (Reprise)), skips the first 1.5 minutes of Act 2, and the smalls may glitch such that the last section of Act 1 doesn't play at all. The 4.07 GB file has worse video quality but does have a working menu, and includes the playbill and various extras (TV spots, Macy's special, Seth's Broadway Chatterbox).
,

Wicked | Broadway | 2019-03-01 | StarCuffedJeans | video

Cast: Laurel Harris (s/b Elphaba), Katie Rose Clarke (Glinda), Ryan McCartan (Fiyero), Michael McCormick (The Wizard), Nancy Opel (Madame Morrible), Gizel Jimenez (Nessarose), Jesse JP Johnson (Boq), Jamie Jackson (Doctor Dillamond), Manuel Herrera (Chistery), Kathy Santen (Midwife), Sterling Masters (Witch's Mother), William Ryall (Witch's Father), William Ryall (Ozian Official)
Notes:
This is a vivid 4K video with almost no obstructions. Pretty much everything is centered, with beautiful zooms but also wider shots that showcase the dancing and set design. At times the video appears on an angle because my wrists are weak, but you don't miss anything because of it. There is also washout at times, but I do believe my camera handles the spotlights better than in a lot of Wicked videos. Act 2 starts a minute into the performance. All in all, this is a gorgeous capture of old and new cast members... I'm not finished yet in this bootleg business but if I was, this could be my magnum opus.
,

Wicked | Broadway | 2019-09-01 | StarCuffedJeans | video

Cast: Hannah Corneau (Elphaba), Brittney Johnson (s/b Glinda), Kyle Dean Massey (t/r Fiyero), Michael McCormick (The Wizard), Nancy Opel (Madame Morrible), Gizel Jimenez (Nessarose), Jesse JP Johnson (Boq), Jamie Jackson (Doctor Dillamond), Chase Madigan (Chistery), Christianne Tisdale (Midwife), Courtney Iventosch (Witch's Mother)
Notes:
Excellent HD capture of Broadway's first Black Glinda and the first Elphaba to have never played the role before in over half a decade! A very Elphaba and Glinda-centric video, it's filmed from the left orchestra with a mix of wides, mediums, and many closeups, with occasional dropouts due to ushers. A bit shaky throughout. Both acts start a minute in. Please do not post screenshots of this video on Twitter ever. Gifs on Tumblr are okay after the NFT date, but don't go linking things to actors and shows.

American Psycho | Kokandy Productions | 2023-10-01 | allisforgiven | video

Cast: Kyle Patrick (Patrick Bateman), Sonia Goldberg (Jean), John Drea (Paul Owen), Amber Dow (Mrs. Bateman), Evan B. Smith (David Van Patten), Quinn Kelch (Luis Carruthers), Anna Seibert (Victoria), Emily Holland (Sabrina), Kevin Parra (Sean Bateman), Caleigh Pan-Kita (Evelyn Williams), Hailey Brisard (Vanden), Will Lidke (Timothy Price), Quinn Simmons (Christine), Johnathan Allsop (Craig McDermott), Danielle Smith (Courtney Lawrence), Ryan Armstrong (Detective Donald Kimball)
Notes:
Considering the circumstances, this is a great capture of the Chicago premiere of this show. This production was staged on a runway down the middle of a large room. Audience was seated on both sides of the stage and actors were frequently in all of the aisles. As a result, actors backs are sometimes facing the camera and ensemble actors sometimes obscure the main action in a scene. Because of the layout, it was impossible to capture the entire stage/runway, so only the middle of the runway is filmed. Unfortunately Act Two was very dark so, while most of the action is there, sometimes the picture is less than stellar from the attempt to lighten the footage enough to see anything. Lastly, lots of reactions can be heard from the woman next to me (she was drunk and had several friends in the show so was super vocal). Despite the aforementioned issues, it's a pretty good video and perfectly watchable.
,

Beautiful 4K capture of the San Francisco company with the post-shutdown script. It's filmed in 16:9 with a mix of wides, mediums, and closeups that beautifully capture the shows magic. This is a great video with excellent sound. Includes the speech by Idina. This bootleg is a treasure. Multiple copies are circulating. The best is the 7.8 GB file, which has higher video resolution, working menus, and the playbill. The 7.63 GB file has the same video quality but no playbill, skips 1 minute in late Act 1 (A Sentimental Man (Reprise)), skips the first 1.5 minutes of Act 2, and the smalls may glitch such that the last section of Act 1 doesn't play at all. The 4.07 GB file has worse video quality but does have a working menu, and includes the playbill and various extras (TV spots, Macy's special, Seth's Broadway Chatterbox).
,

Wicked | Broadway | 2019-03-01 | StarCuffedJeans | video

Notes:
This is a vivid 4K video with almost no obstructions. Pretty much everything is centered, with beautiful zooms but also wider shots that showcase the dancing and set design. At times the video appears on an angle because my wrists are weak, but you don't miss anything because of it. There is also washout at times, but I do believe my camera handles the spotlights better than in a lot of Wicked videos. Act 2 starts a minute into the performance. All in all, this is a gorgeous capture of old and new cast members... I'm not finished yet in this bootleg business but if I was, this could be my magnum opus.

American Psycho | Kokandy Productions | 2023-10-01 | allisforgiven | video

Cast: Kyle Patrick (Patrick Bateman), Sonia Goldberg (Jean), John Drea (Paul Owen), Amber Dow (Mrs. Bateman), Evan B. Smith (David Van Patten), Quinn Kelch (Luis Carruthers), Anna Seibert (Victoria), Emily Holland (Sabrina), Kevin Parra (Sean Bateman), Caleigh Pan-Kita (Evelyn Williams), Hailey Brisard (Vanden), Will Lidke (Timothy Price), Quinn Simmons (Christine), Johnathan Allsop (Craig McDermott), Danielle Smith (Courtney Lawrence), Ryan Armstrong (Detective Donald Kimball)
Notes:
Considering the circumstances, this is a great capture of the Chicago premiere of this show. This production was staged on a runway down the middle of a large room. Audience was seated on both sides of the stage and actors were frequently in all of the aisles. As a result, actors backs are sometimes facing the camera and ensemble actors sometimes obscure the main action in a scene. Because of the layout, it was impossible to capture the entire stage/runway, so only the middle of the runway is filmed. Unfortunately Act Two was very dark so, while most of the action is there, sometimes the picture is less than stellar from the attempt to lighten the footage enough to see anything. Lastly, lots of reactions can be heard from the woman next to me (she was drunk and had several friends in the show so was super vocal). Despite the aforementioned issues, it's a pretty good video and perfectly watchable.
,

Hadestown | Broadway | 2022-02-19 | musain | video

Cast: Reeve Carney (Orpheus), Eva Noblezada (Eurydice), Amber Gray (Persephone), Patrick Page (Hades), André De Shields (Hermes), Tara Jackson (u/s Fate), Jewelle Blackman (Fate), Kay Trinidad (Fate), Emily Afton (Worker), Malcolm Armwood (Worker), Timothy Hughes (Worker), Grace Yoo (Worker), Trent Saunders (Worker)
Notes:
Amber Gray's final performance in Hadestown. Full show is filmed, including the standing ovation that Amber got before the performance even started, right up to the band exiting. Moderate obstruction from the box/bar, etc. Dropouts and shakiness during applause breaks, especially during all of the standing ovations that happened for Amber—what can I say? It was such an emotional night and I was more focused on being in the moment than getting a 4K video. However, what is captured is high quality, and is of a very memorable show. For transparency, some screenshots include the obstructed/less-than-HQ moments, so people know what they're purchasing/watching. Band: Brian Drye (Trombone), Marika Hughes (Cello), Dana Lyn (Violin), Ben Perowsky (Drums), Robinson Morse (Bass), Ilusha Tsinadze (Guitar), Liam Robinson (Keys)

Notes:
Beautiful 4K capture of the San Francisco company with the post-shutdown script. It's filmed in 16:9 with a mix of wides, mediums, and closeups that beautifully capture the shows magic. There's some minor obstructions: the balcony railing can be seen at the bottom during wides and when the action takes place all the way at the front, and a head can be seen at the bottom right corner. There's almost no washout and wandering is minimal, but during darker scenes the action can be harder to make out. The sound is excellent. Includes curtain call and playbill scans.

Wicked | Broadway | 2004-07-18 | Pigerty | video

Cast: Idina Menzel (Elphaba), Kristin Chenoweth (Glinda), Norbert Leo Butz (Fiyero), Sean McCourt (u/s The Wizard), Carole Shelley (Madame Morrible), Michelle Federer (Nessarose), Randy Harrison (t/r Boq), William Youmans (Doctor Dillamond)
Notes:
This is Kristin and Norbert's last show. It was also supposed to be Joel Grey's last show, but he was ill. Video is sound only for the first 4 minutes and for the last 30 seconds of Defying Gravity. This is a great video with excellent sound. Includes the speech by Idina. This bootleg is a treasure. Multiple copies are circulating. The best is the 7.8 GB file, which has higher video resolution, working menus, and the playbill. The 7.63 GB file has the same video quality but no playbill, skips 1 minute in late Act 1 (A Sentimental Man (Reprise)), skips the first 1.5 minutes of Act 2, and the smalls may glitch such that the last section of Act 1 doesn't play at all. The 4.07 GB file has worse video quality but does have a working menu, and includes the playbill and various extras (TV spots, Macy's special, Seth's Broadway Chatterbox).
,

Wicked | Broadway | 2013-05-12 | Lanelle | video

Cast: Willemijn Verkaik (Elphaba), Katie Rose Clarke (Glinda), Kyle Dean Massey (Fiyero), Adam Grupper (The Wizard), Randy Danson (Madame Morrible), Catherine Charlebois (Nessarose), F. Michael Haynie (Boq), John Schiappa (Doctor Dillamond)
Notes:
Filmed from the right orchestra, at a slight angle, but excellent quality. The taper originally released this as a blu-ray, 2-disc DVDs or 1-disc DVD, so make sure to get the version that best suits your needs.

Wicked | Broadway | 2019-03-01 | StarCuffedJeans | video

Cast: Laurel Harris (s/b Elphaba), Katie Rose Clarke (Glinda), Ryan McCartan (Fiyero), Michael McCormick (The Wizard), Nancy Opel (Madame Morrible), Gizel Jimenez (Nessarose), Jesse JP Johnson (Boq), Jamie Jackson (Doctor Dillamond), Manuel Herrera (Chistery), Kathy Santen (Midwife), Sterling Masters (Witch's Mother), William Ryall (Witch's Father), William Ryall (Ozian Official)
Notes:
This is a vivid 4K video with almost no obstructions. Pretty much everything is centered, with beautiful zooms but also wider shots that showcase the dancing and set design. At times the video appears on an angle because my wrists are weak, but you don't miss anything because of it. There is also washout at times, but I do believe my camera handles the spotlights better than in a lot of Wicked videos. Act 2 starts a minute into the performance. All in all, this is a gorgeous capture of old and new cast members... I'm not finished yet in this bootleg business but if I was, this could be my magnum opus.
,

Wicked | Broadway | 2019-09-01 | StarCuffedJeans | video

Cast: Hannah Corneau (Elphaba), Brittney Johnson (s/b Glinda), Kyle Dean Massey (t/r Fiyero), Michael McCormick (The Wizard), Nancy Opel (Madame Morrible), Gizel Jimenez (Nessarose), Jesse JP Johnson (Boq), Jamie Jackson (Doctor Dillamond), Chase Madigan (Chistery), Christianne Tisdale (Midwife), Courtney Iventosch (Witch's Mother)
Notes:
Excellent HD capture of Broadway's first Black Glinda and the first Elphaba to have never played the role before in over half a decade! A very Elphaba and Glinda-centric video, it's filmed from the left orchestra with a mix of wides, mediums, and many closeups, with occasional dropouts due to ushers. A bit shaky throughout. Both acts start a minute in. Please do not post screenshots of this video on Twitter ever. Gifs on Tumblr are okay after the NFT date, but don't go linking things to actors and shows.
